Selected Speeches of Reverend Sun Myung Moon

Compiled by the Committee for the Collection of Reverend Sun Myung Moon's Speeches

Foreword
                   President of the Family Federation for World Peace and Unification  Hwang Sun Jo
Reverend Sun Myung Moon, who received the calling for the salvation of humanity from Heaven at the age of 16, has lived his entire life centered on the Heavenly Way with a single-minded devotion. He described his life as follows:
"If Reverend Moon has any assets, it is the suffering endured for public purposes rather than for personal hardship; that is my only asset. In social life, I tried to suffer more than anyone else. In the providential position, I also tried to suffer more than anyone else. ... Reverend Moon has been opposed and persecuted by the nation and the world. He was opposed in America, by Christianity, Judaism, and even communism. Never in history has the world united to attack one person with the intent to eliminate him. In this sense, Reverend Moon is a global champion. 
However, despite being cursed, he has not been destroyed or perished. He has emerged even stronger without the slightest tremor. ... Reverend Moon advocates for the liberation of humanity, the spiritual world, hell, and even God." (Refer to the Collection of Speeches, Volume 105, pages 101-103)
In a word, Reverend Moon's life can be defined as 'suffering itself.' The nature of this suffering is not for himself but for God and humanity. From this, we come to know who he is. Reverend Moon is the Messiah and Savior that Christianity has hoped for over 2,000 years, and he has come as the True Parent of humanity. Already, disciples in 185 countries around the world are striving to walk the path of true children by realizing the ideal of the true family with such a confession of faith.
Reverend Moon's identity is verified through his words and life. He possesses a truth not found in the world. The issues of God and humanity, history, and the world are clarified through his words. The promise of the new word prophesied in the Bible is fulfilled in him, setting us free. These words contain 'vitality.' Moreover, the more important aspect is that Reverend Moon's words are merely an 'interpretation of his own life.' In other words, he himself is the truth. The Word became flesh, that is, he incarnated. Therefore, life itself is truth, and it approaches us through the framework of 'the Word.'
I am confident that readers will understand his greatness through Reverend Moon's words. Although the level of Reverend Moon's words is too high and deep to fully comprehend, they fundamentally have three characteristics.
First, Reverend Moon revealed God through his words and life. He liberated God from silence and suffering. The pain of God, who cannot call His children His own due to their evil lineage, and the sorrow of God, who was tragically alienated due to human sin, were made to 'speak' by Reverend Moon. He made God, who was silent within the confines of church authority, doctrine, and ornate buildings, 'speak,' and he made God, who could not come as a parent, 'become a parent,' thus Reverend Moon is 'the complete revelation of God.'
Second, Reverend Moon liberated humanity from ignorance and chaos. Although we humans have the ability to think and make value judgments, we cannot deny the tragic reality that we cannot fully explain our own existence. Furthermore, although humans are not independent beings and are interdependent with others, they have not been able to explain that relationship. The reason is that we lost God's word. Reverend Moon provides the ultimate answer to this. Moreover, through a life that upholds the Heavenly Way, he shows a concrete model path. Therefore, his words are living words full of life.
Third, Reverend Moon liberated the world of all things. Every object created by God has its unique value as an individual truth body. Although its value should be fully realized by receiving the original human dominion, it has not been, and thus all things have groaned. Reverend Moon clarified the original value of the world of all things through his words and opened the way for ultimate reconciliation between humans and all things by restoring humans to their original state.
Reverend Moon and his wife, who came as the eternal True Parents of humanity, continue to tirelessly speak to the world, urging us to 'serve with the heart of a parent and the body of a servant,' and to 'live for others,' striving to inherit true love, true life, and true lineage. I hope that readers who encounter these words will share in this grace. *

It is also an issue in the spirit world, but what is the solution? You must offer devotion and meet Mohammed through the spirit world and have a Q&A. If it is true, if they oppose it, that country will be completely destroyed. You don't have to worry about such things now.  
Once the nation is found, the content of the Unification Church will be broadcast every day. There is nothing more to broadcast than that. All the facts of the spirit world will be revealed. Unknown incidents like the assassination of President Kennedy will also be revealed by calling Kennedy and having a Q&A. Such facts will be testified to.  
All the national secrets and suspicious incidents of the world will be unfolded as they are. Do you understand what I mean? "Yes." You call them and have a Q&A. Do you understand? "Yes." If the king of the Muslims opposes, you call the ancestors and have them testify. "Call anyone you trust and have a Q&A," and ask how they will answer these facts, asking about things only they know, asking the spirit.  
You ask how they think about this, and how they did something in that village, and with just three questions, they will raise their hands. Do you understand what I mean? That time is coming. When the teacher went to Pyongyang in the past, he was rumored to be a shaman. They said not to catch Reverend Moon. Do you understand what I mean? They crawled. So, you correct everything as a person. If you did it with the history of the spirit, it would end in one generation.  
We Must Move the UN  
The teacher's teaching is eternal truth. Do you understand? You must pray for that. Isn't it the same for our blessed families? How do you attach someone as a partner when your ideal partner, someone you are meeting for the first time, is standing there, and the teacher blesses them? How do you attach them? I said this two years ago. The teacher's hands and feet know. Even now, it's the same.  
Even now, but I don't say such things. The teacher is not a strange person. It is done logically. An American young man said, "I will become the king of an island nation!" but there was a well-looking woman from that country, and I found her and matched them as partners. So, they were surprised. "Teacher, how did you match them so well?" I don't know either. Do you understand?  
Therefore, if you say something is wrong or dislike what the teacher did...
It is to drive oneself to the point of death. Absolutely. If I don't do what my heart desires, the indemnity is great. If I say one wrong word, I must repent. It's about teaching. You can't live recklessly. You can't live moderately. You must live on earth while adhering to the laws of heaven. You all don't know, do you? You don't know how to live, do you? You don't know the content that makes it possible, do you? Without the content and the people who can do that, the world cannot be managed. That's why, looking at the facts of my life, I see that the divorce was insufficient.

How much would God want to reveal that? It was prophesied 450 years ago, even mentioning the Moon family. God's firstborn is the Moon family. There are twelve or so things, and somehow they were drawn exactly about the teacher. Even looking at that, does the teacher qualify as the True Parent, the Messiah, or not? "He does." What qualifies? I think it doesn't. If you think it does, how much higher must you go? I think it doesn't, and there is still much to be done.

Okay, that's enough for today. We didn't have a reading session. "The reading book was earlier..." Not that, let's do "Father's Prayer." "We've been doing 'Father's Prayer' all along." There were many times when Father cried, right? "We did the reading session with many tears." How many pages are there? When Father prayed or spoke, it was at the moment of life and death, a place of deciding whether to live or die. If I die tomorrow, it must appear in the words and in the prayers. Words spoken 50 years ago are being spoken now. You never know when you will die. There are so many enemies. There are many here, too. How dangerous a place is this? Who did you trust to come here? Did you trust the people here? How can you trust those who, when they are tired, go into their rooms to sleep and leave the teacher behind, running away?

Here, Paraguay is a place where criminals come to escape. When people from Argentina or Brazil commit crimes, they come here because no one lives here, and it's a refuge. The reason I told you to form teams of three people here is to create many people so that you can know such information and talk about it when you get closer. Also, if you set it up here, even if you come again in the future, you won't have to pay for food, just find three people anywhere. They will try to host a feast for you and invite you to stay at their house. Isn't that great?

You don't really understand what the teacher is saying now, do you? Now, you must move the UN. You must move the UN. The time is approaching urgently. That's why yesterday, I gave all the instructions for that. You never know what might happen.

Do you know when someone will die? It's the same. You shouldn't think that today or yesterday or forever is the same day. Sometimes you go over a mountain peak, sometimes you cross a valley, sometimes you cross a bridge. You never know when Satan will appear as an ambush to strike you.

Fulfill the Responsibility of Blessing

Today, there were so many mosquitoes, I've never been bitten by mosquitoes like that before. Yoon Sang! "Yes." Did you see it for the first time today? We caught four in five minutes there. What did we catch? We caught pacu. How many over 60 cm? Three? No, five.

If we go there tomorrow, we'll catch a lot. "Where..." (Laughter) I'll guide you. (Laughter) They're everywhere. They're everywhere. You just can't see them. You just can't attach the bait. These days, it's the time when fish come in. What do you do with catching a lot? It's just busy. (Recording briefly cuts) "We caught 68." In how many days? "If we catch them tomorrow, it will be over." You played around. (Laughter) Even catching 680 would barely earn praise. How will you make a living with that? "We caught 160 in three years." How will you make a living with that? (Laughter) You have to think about making a living. "Since we practiced, we'll catch a lot next time." Ah, three days of practice should be enough, what is there to practice? The problem is not the fish biting, but catching them all. The reason you can't catch fish is that you lack the skill to hook them.

Your fishing rods are like this. You have to see where the fishing rod bends. Do you understand? When it bends like this, you have to pull it like this, and when it bends like that, you have to pull it like that. You lose the fish in the gap of one inch bending. You don't know how skilled they are. You have to teach a lot of secrets. Big ones like boga don't bite suddenly. They do this. They do this and then just eat one leg. They eat the crab legs one by one in order. There's a slight difference. Once they've eaten all the legs, they eat the body, but at that time, they hold it for a long time without hooking it. So when the big shell and legs are in, you have to hook it. To catch a big one, what should you do? Big ones know whether they will live or die. You have to know how much they've suffered. Big ones have been caught on hooks once or twice and have experienced life and death. They've been caught on hooks many times. If the mouth is torn, it's because it was caught on a hook, not bitten and torn.

It's the same with pacu. Among the big ones, there are many experienced ones. With dorado, I've caught so many... In one day, I catch eighteen, twenty-one, like that. I've lost interest. I usually caught fifteen, so it would be nice to take them. These days, it's not possible, you have to wait a little longer. In December, it's when they lay eggs and grow, and if you go then, it's abundant.

The teacher doesn't look like someone who knows how to fish, right? Doesn't he look dull? Does he look dull or sharp? That's why, as much as you want... Religious leaders are like that. Even a slight difference in air becomes self-reproach. It's that sensitive.

Kim Young-hwi! "Yes." Shouldn't you share the feast from your 60th birthday? "Yes." Are you planning to eat alone for your 70th birthday? (Laughter) Gwang-ryeol! Yoo Gwang-ryeol! "Yes." You're the same. "I woke up and it was my 70th birthday." Preparing for tomorrow, how wonderful it is, don't do things that turn into waste while sleeping, work and be grateful for the time given to catch fish. So, Yoo Gwang-ryeol doesn't want it, so it's okay not to eat. "Even tomorrow, formally..." Tomorrow is not necessary. Even if the teacher said it today, if you give it your way, I won't accept it. Absolute obedience, right? Absolute faith? "Yes." Ah, Yoo Gwang-ryeol, I mean. Is it absolute obedience or what? "Absolute submission." What is absolute submission? (Laughter) So where are you going?

So, share one each. I don't know if it will go around. It might not go around, so just do one each, and if there's any left, then all... "It was given by Father." It was given by Mother. "Everyone, applause!" (Applause) I was planning to catch a cow and feed it, but there's no time. Catching a cow here is not a problem. It's simple. If you give 200 dollars, they take care of everything, and if you give 270 dollars, they even cut it for you. Would it be good to catch a cow tomorrow? "Yes. There's a lot of meat caught a few days ago." "Catch another one." There are two cows here, so instead of catching one, catch both. Is it three? "Yes." I'm fine. Share this. "There are a lot here." Even if there are many, I don't know if it will go around. "There are a lot here."

This time, because I couldn't fulfill the responsibility of blessing, when I go back, I have to finish it like lightning. Does it go around? "Yes, there are leftovers." "Thank you for the meal."
